		#		AND = { has_country_flag = harm_army_focus OR = { has_tech = basic_heavy_tank has_tech = improved_heavy_tank has_tech = advanced_heavy_tank } NOT = { ai_has_role_template = heavy_armor } }
        #
		#		AND = { has_country_flag = at_design_AT has_tech = interwar_antitank NOT = { ai_has_role_template = at_infantry } }
		#		AND = { has_country_flag = at_design_MTD OR = { has_tech = basic_medium_td has_tech = improved_medium_td has_tech = advanced_medium_td } NOT = { ai_has_role_template = at_infantry } }
		#		AND = { has_country_flag = at_design_HTD OR = { has_tech = basic_heavy_td has_tech = improved_heavy_td has_tech = advanced_heavy_td } NOT = { ai_has_role_template = at_infantry } }
		#	}
		#}

		#EVENT TEMPLATE FIX
		modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = garrison_template } }

		#FIX
		modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = garrison_rotation } }
	}
	match_to_count = 0.95

	######################################################## design A (inf+art)

	################### normal design
	sf_infantry_template_A_regular_RART = {
		upgrade_prio = {
			factor = 3

			#DESIGN REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = infantry_design_A } }

			#DATE REQ.
			#modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { date > 1938.1.1 } }

			#DOCTRINE REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = sf_doctrine } }

			#TECH REQ.
			#modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_tech = rocket_artillery } }

			#ARMY FOCUS REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 OR = { has_country_flag = infantry_attachment_1 has_country_flag = infantry_attachment_2 } }

			#ADVISOR REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 prefer_artillery_design = yes }
		}
		production_prio = {
			factor = 3

			#DESIGN REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = infantry_design_A } }

			#DATE REQ.
			#modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { date > 1938.1.1 } }

			#DOCTRINE REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = sf_doctrine } }

			#TECH REQ.
			#modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_tech = rocket_artillery } }

			#ARMY FOCUS REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 OR = { has_country_flag = infantry_attachment_1 has_country_flag = infantry_attachment_2 } }

			#ADVISOR REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 prefer_artillery_design = yes }
		}

		#can_upgrade_in_field = {}

		#replace_at_match =
		#replace_with =
		#target_min_match =

		reinforce_prio = 1
		#custom_icon =

		#TEMPLATE
		target_width = 27
		width_weight = 1
		column_swap_factor = 1

		target_template = {
			weight = 1
			match_value = 1000

			regiments = {
				infantry = 9
				artillery_brigade = 3
			}

			support = {
				engineer = 1

	sf_at_infantry_template_AT_1 = {

	########## AT design design
	mw_at_infantry_template_AT_1 = {
		upgrade_prio = {
			factor = 1

			#DOCTRINE REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = mw_doctrine } }

			#ARMY FOCUS REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = infantry_army_focus } }

			#DESIGN REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = at_design_AT } }

			#ENEMY ARMOR INTEL REQ.
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0 
				OR = { 
					any_neighbor_country = { ROOT = { estimated_intel_max_armor = { tag = PREV value > 50 } } }
					any_enemy_country = { ROOT = { estimated_intel_max_armor = { tag = PREV value > 50 } } }

	gb_at_infantry_template_AT_1 = {

			factor = 1

			#ARMY FOCUS REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = infantry_army_focus } }

			#DESIGN REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = at_design_AT } }

			#ENEMY ARMOR INTEL REQ.
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0 
				OR = { 
					any_neighbor_country = { ROOT = { estimated_intel_max_armor = { tag = PREV value > 50 } } }

	########## AT design design
	ma_at_regular_infantry_template_AT_1 = {
		upgrade_prio = {
			factor = 1

			#DOCTRINE REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = ma_doctrine } }

			#DESIGN REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = at_design_AT } }

			#ENEMY ARMOR INTEL REQ.
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0 
				OR = { 
					any_neighbor_country = { ROOT = { estimated_intel_max_armor = { tag = PREV value > 50 } } }
					any_enemy_country = { ROOT = { estimated_intel_max_armor = { tag = PREV value > 50 } } }
				} 
			}
			
			#TECH REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 OR = { has_tech = human_wave_offensive has_tech = vast_offensives } }
		}
		production_prio = {
			factor = 1

			#DOCTRINE REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = ma_doctrine } }

				anti_tank = 1
			}
		}

			#REGIMENTS
			infantry
			artillery_brigade
			anti_tank_brigade
